## ZIMError

Error infomation

**Details**

Error infomation.

*Declared in `ZIMDefines.h`*

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="code"
  prototype="@property ZIMErrorCode code"
  parent_name="ZIMError"
  parent_type="class">
Description: The storage path of the log files. Refer to the official website document for the default path.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="message"
  prototype="@property NSString *message"
  parent_name="ZIMError"
  parent_type="class">
Description: Error infomation description.
</ParamField>

  parent_name="ZIMAppConfig"

</ParamField>

## ZIMLogConfig

Log configuration

**Details**

Configure the storage path of log files and the maximum log file size.

*Declared in `ZIMDefines.h`*

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="logPath"
  prototype="@property NSString *logPath"
  parent_name="ZIMLogConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The storage path of the log files. Refer to the official website document for the default path.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="logSize"
  prototype="@property unsigned long long logSize"
  parent_name="ZIMLogConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The maximum log file size (Bytes). The default maximum size is 5MB (5 * 1024 * 1024 Bytes)
</ParamField>

## ZIMCacheConfig

Cache configuration

**Details**

Configure the storage path of cache files (such as chat records).

*Declared in `ZIMDefines.h`*

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="cachePath"
  prototype="@property NSString *cachePath"
  parent_name="ZIMCacheConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The storage path of the cache files. Refer to the official website document for the default path.
</ParamField>

## ZIMUserInfo

User information object.

**Details**

Identifies a unique user.

*Declared in `ZIMDefines.h`*

<Note title="">
- **Caution**：Note that the userID must be unique under the same appID, otherwise mutual kicks out will occur. It is strongly recommended that userID corresponds to the user ID of the business APP, that is, a userID and a real user are fixed and unique, and should not be passed to the SDK in a random userID. Because the unique and fixed userID allows ZEGO technicians to quickly locate online problems.
</Note>

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="userID"
  prototype="@property NSString *userID"
  parent_name="ZIMUserInfo"
  parent_type="class">
User ID, a string with a maximum length of 32 bytes or less. It is customized by the developer. Only support numbers, English characters and  '!', '#', '$', '%', '&', '(', ')', '+', '-', ':', ';', '\<', '=', '.', '\>', '?', '@', '[', ']', '^', '_', '\{', '\}', '|', '~'.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="userName"
  prototype="@property NSString *userName"
  parent_name="ZIMUserInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Description: User name, defined by you. For version 2.0.0 and onwards, the string has a maximum length of 256 bytes.Required: Not required.Privacy reminder: Please do not provide sensitive personal information, including but not limited to mobile phone numbers, ID card numbers, passport numbers, and real names.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="userAvatarUrl"
  prototype="@property NSString *userAvatarUrl"

## ZIMUserFullInfo

User full information object.

**Details**

Identifies a unique user.

*Declared in `ZIMDefines.h`*

<Note title="">
- **Caution**：Note that the userID must be unique under the same appID, otherwise mutual kicks out will occur. It is strongly recommended that userID corresponds to the user ID of the business APP, that is, a userID and a real user are fixed and unique, and should not be passed to the SDK in a random userID. Because the unique and fixed userID allows ZEGO technicians to quickly locate online problems.
</Note>

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="baseInfo"
  prototype="@property [ZIMUserInfo](./class#zimuserinfo) baseInfo"
  parent_name="ZIMUserFullInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Description: User basic information.
</ParamField>

User information query configuration, you can choose to query from the local or from the server. Query the unlimited frequency constraints from the local, and query the limited frequency constraints from the server. You can only query the detailed configuration of 10 users within 10 s.

</ParamField>

## ZIMOfflinePushPrivateMessageTemplate

The private message template is currently only applicable to the OPPO manufacturer.

**Details**

According to [OPUSH DMS template check ability to access instructions](https://open.oppomobile.com/documentation/page/info?id=12391), OPPO in new message classification on the basis of the new push DMS templates, After you have configured the private message template in the OPPO console, if you need to apply the corresponding template during push notifications, you can assign a value to the privateMessageTemplate in ZIMPushConfig.

*Declared in `ZIMDefines.h`*

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="templateID"
  prototype="@property NSString *templateID"
  parent_name="ZIMOfflinePushPrivateMessageTemplate"
  parent_type="class">
Description: The private message template ID is currently only applicable to OPPO manufacturers. Please fill in the template ID preset in the OPPO Open Platform console.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="titleParameters"
  prototype="@property NSString *titleParameters"
  parent_name="ZIMOfflinePushPrivateMessageTemplate"
  parent_type="class">
Description: To replace the content of the preset title field in the template, a json string needs to be filled in, such as "\{"user_name":" Li Hua "\}".
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="contentParameters"
  prototype="@property NSString *contentParameters"
  parent_name="ZIMOfflinePushPrivateMessageTemplate"
  parent_type="class">
Description: To replace the content of the preset fields in the template, a json string needs to be filled in, such as "\{"city":" Shenzhen "\}".
</ParamField>

<Note title="">

## ZIMMediaMessage

Base class for media message objects.

**Details**

Identifies a media message.

*Declared in `ZIMDefines.h`*

<Note title="">
- **Caution**：This base class is the basis of all media messages and contains the properties required by media messages.
</Note>

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="fileLocalPath"
  prototype="@property NSString *fileLocalPath"
  parent_name="ZIMMediaMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The local path of the media message. Required: If a local file is sent, this parameter must be set by the sender. Otherwise, the message fails to be sent.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileDownloadUrl"
  prototype="@property NSString *fileDownloadUrl"
  parent_name="ZIMMediaMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The external download url of the media message is used for the developer to transparently transmit the media file to other users by filling in this URL when the developer uploads the media file to his own server.Required or not: If an external URL is sent, this parameter is mandatory on the sender end.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileUID"
  prototype="@property NSString *fileUID"
  parent_name="ZIMMediaMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The unique ID of the media file. Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in, this value is generated by the SDK.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileName"
  prototype="@property NSString *fileName"
  parent_name="ZIMMediaMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The filename of the media file. Required or not: If you are sending an external URL, you need to fill in this value and include the file extension. If a local file is sent, the value is optional.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileSize"
  prototype="@property long long fileSize"
  parent_name="ZIMMediaMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The size of the media file. Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in, this value is generated by the SDK.
</ParamField>

## ZIMMessageSendNotification

The notification callback when the message is sent, you can get the relevant information before the message object is sent through this notification

**Details**

Through this notification, developers can obtain relevant information before the message object is sent, such as localMessageID, etc.

*Declared in `ZIMDefines.h`*

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**：When developers need to record and cache relevant information before sending a message, they can obtain it by listening to the notification.
- **Caution**：If no monitoring is required, it can be passed [null].
</Note>

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="onMessageAttached"
  prototype="@property [ZIMMessageAttachedCallback](./class#zimmessageattachedcallback) onMessageAttached"
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSendNotification"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: After the message falls into the local DB, the notification will be called back before the message is sent to the server. Business scenario: This interface can be used when the developer needs to obtain the relevant information in the message in advance before sending the message. Required: not required. If no monitoring is required, it can be passed empty. Default: empty.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="onMediaUploadingProgress"
  prototype="@property [ZIMMediaUploadingProgress](./class#zimmediauploadingprogress) onMediaUploadingProgress"
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSendNotification"
  parent_type="class">
Description: Media file upload progress.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="onMultipleMediaUploadingProgress"
  prototype="@property [ZIMMultipleMediaUploadingProgress](./class#zimmultiplemediauploadingprogress) onMultipleMediaUploadingProgress"
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSendNotification"
  parent_type="class">
Description: Multiple media file upload progress.
</ParamField>

## ZIMMessageSearchConfig

Message search configuration.

**Details**

Message search configuration.

*Declared in `ZIMDefines.h`*

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="nextMessage"
  prototype="@property [ZIMMessage](./class#zimmessage) nextMessage"
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Paging fetch flag, which means fetching messages before or after nextMessage, with 'before' or 'after' determined by the order value. On the first search, nextMessage is null. On subsequent searches, nextMessage needs to pass in the last message in the message list queried last time.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="count"
  prototype="@property unsigned int count"
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
count It is recommended to keep the number of items less than 20 to reduce performance overhead.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="order"
  prototype="@property [ZIMMessageOrder](./enum#zimmessageorder) order"
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
When the 'order' is 'DESCENDING' during message search, it means querying messages with sending time earlier than nextMessage. If it's the first message query (i.e. nextMessage is null), then query from the last message stored locally forward. When 'order' is 'ASCENDING', it means querying messages with sending time later than nextMessage. If it's the first message query (i.e. nextMessage is null), then query from the first message stored locally backward. The default is 'DESCENDING'.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="keywords"
  prototype="@property NSArray<NSString *> *keywords"
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Search keywords, up to 5 keywords are supported, otherwise an error will be reported. For example: passing in '1' and '2' will make the search results only show messages that contain both keywords '1' and '2'.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="messageTypes"
  prototype="@property NSArray<[ZIMMessageType](./enum#zimmessagetype) *> *messageTypes"
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Message types, can be used to specify message types. Support passing in multiple types.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="subMessageTypes"
  prototype="@property NSArray<unsigned int *> *subMessageTypes"
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The subtypes of custom messages have a value range of [0,200]. Developers can use this range to search for specific custom types.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="senderUserIDs"
  prototype="@property NSArray<NSString *> *senderUserIDs"
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The user ID of the message sender, supporting up to 5 IDs. For example, if 'zego2023' is passed in, the search results will only display all the messages sent by the user 'zego2023' in that conversation.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="startTime"
  prototype="@property long long startTime"
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The starting point of the search, in milliseconds, with a default value of 0. The format is UTC timestamp.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="endTime"
  prototype="@property long long endTime"
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The ending point of the search, which must be greater than the startTime, in milliseconds. The default value is 0 and the format is UTC timestamp.
</ParamField>

## ZIMMessageRepliedListQueryConfig

Configuration for querying reply message list.

**Details**

Configuration class for querying the replied message list.

*Declared in `ZIMDefines.h`*

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="nextFlag"
  prototype="@property long long nextFlag"
  parent_name="ZIMMessageRepliedListQueryConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The flag of paginated query. When querying for the first time, set this field to 0. If the 'nextFlag' field of the [queryMessageRepliedList] callback is not 0, it means that the query has not ended yet. You need to set it here to continue querying the next page.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="count"
  prototype="@property unsigned int count"
  parent_name="ZIMMessageRepliedListQueryConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The number of queries per query. The upper limit is 100. Exceeding 100 will result in an error.
</ParamField>

## ZIMConversationSearchConfig

Conversation search configuration.

**Details**

Conversation search configuration.

*Declared in `ZIMDefines.h`*

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="mode"
  prototype="@property [ZIMConversationSearchMode](./enum#zimconversationsearchmode) mode"
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Conversation search mode.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="nextFlag"
  prototype="@property unsigned int nextFlag"
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Pagination token, fill in 0 initially, and then fill in the nextFlag returned from the callback to retrieve data for the next page.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="totalConversationCount"
  prototype="@property unsigned int totalConversationCount"
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The number of messages that can be retrieved in one search. It is recommended to be less than 20 to reduce performance overhead.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="keywords"
  prototype="@property NSArray<NSString *> *keywords"
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Search keywords, supports up to 5. Otherwise, an error will occur. For example, if you pass in '1' and '2', the search results will only display conversations that contain both '1' and '2' keywords in the messages.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="conversationMessageCount"
  prototype="@property unsigned int conversationMessageCount"
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The number of local messages that can be retrieved for a single conversation in one search. It is recommended to be less than 10 to reduce performance overhead.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="messageTypes"
  prototype="@property NSArray<[ZIMMessageType](./enum#zimmessagetype) *> *messageTypes"
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Message types, can be used to specify message types. Support passing in multiple types.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="subMessageTypes"
  prototype="@property NSArray<unsigned int *> *subMessageTypes"
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The subtypes of custom messages have a value range of [0,200]. Developers can use this range to search for specific custom types.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="senderUserIDs"
  prototype="@property NSArray<NSString *> *senderUserIDs"
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Send user ID, supports up to 5. For example, if you pass in zego2023, the search results will only display conversations where messages have been sent by the user zego2023.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="startTime"
  prototype="@property long long startTime"
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The starting point of the search, in milliseconds, with a default value of 0. The format is UTC timestamp.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="endTime"
  prototype="@property long long endTime"
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The ending point of the search, which must be greater than the startTime, in milliseconds. The default value is 0 and the format is UTC timestamp.
</ParamField>

## ZIMLogUploadedCallback

### Methods
<ParamField
  name="onLogUploaded"
  prototype="void(^[ZIMLogUploadedCallback](#zimloguploadedcallback))(([ZIMError](./class#zimerror)) errorInfo);"
  desc="Callback of the log upload result."
  parent_name="ZIMLogUploadedCallback">

**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| errorInfo | [ZIMError](./class#zimerror) | Error code information, used to obtain the result of the interface call. code is 0 for success, and non-0 for failure. When an interface call fails, developers should check the error code documentation on the official website for solutions. |

</ParamField>

## ZIMLoggedInCallback

### Methods
<ParamField
  name="onLoggedIn"
  prototype="void(^[ZIMLoggedInCallback](#zimloggedincallback))(([ZIMError](./class#zimerror)) errorInfo);"
  desc="Callback of the login result."
  parent_name="ZIMLoggedInCallback">

**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| errorInfo | [ZIMError](./class#zimerror) | Error code information, used to obtain the result of the interface call. code is 0 for success, and non-0 for failure. When an interface call fails, developers should check the error code documentation on the official website for solutions. |

**Details**

After the developer login, execute the callback of the result.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**：Developers can use the [errorCode] in the callback to determine whether the login is successful.
- **Triggered when**：When the developer calls the [login] interface, the callback will be triggered.
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**：1.2.0 and above.
</Warning>

</ParamField>

## ZIMTokenRenewedCallback

### Methods
<ParamField
  name="onTokenRenewed"
  prototype="void(^[ZIMTokenRenewedCallback](#zimtokenrenewedcallback))((NSString *) token, ([ZIMError](./class#zimerror)) errorInfo);"
  desc="Callback of the result of renewing the token."
  parent_name="ZIMTokenRenewedCallback">

**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| token | NSString * | The renewed token. |

  parent_name="ZIMCommunityMembersMutedCallback">

**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| communityID | NSString * | Community ID. |
| channelID | NSString * | The channel ID. Empty means muted at the community level. |
| isMute | BOOL | Whether to mute the members. |
| errorUserList | NSArray\<[ZIMErrorUserInfo](./class#zimerroruserinfo) *\> * | List of users that failed to be muted. |
| errorInfo | [ZIMError](./class#zimerror) | Error code information, used to obtain the result of the interface call. code is 0 for success, and non-0 for failure. When an interface call fails, developers should check the error code documentation on the official website for solutions. |

</ParamField>
